Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Aviation Competition Fever 233

— Jia Wei

It is said that this time, taking advantage of Australia's centenary, Britain held the greatest aviation competition in history: a grand event with twenty aircraft and dozens of flying generals, from Haddington to Melbourne, in southeastern Australia, a journey of more than 11,300 miles. The British young aviator Scott and Black, the champions, completed this long journey across mountains and rivers in less than three days—only seventy-one hours and eighteen minutes. Such a great and astonishing feat in the history of world transportation is truly worthy of human praise, admiration, and commemoration in grand style.

However, the motives and intentions behind this aviation competition are certainly not that simple. No one can deny that the political and economic foundation of British imperialism in the Far East has been greatly threatened and even shaken since Japanese imperialism launched the "September 18th Incident" and its ambitions erupted. Moreover, today, the world is in a turbulent and eventful time, to the extent that negotiations on the naval ratio, which are closely related to Britain, have failed to produce results, and everyone is at a standstill. Then, an imperialist power with more colonies than its homeland must use all kinds of methods to strengthen the organization of its vast British Empire spread all over the world. Therefore, the launch of this Anglo-Australian aviation competition cannot be said to be its long-planned attempt and intention.

In addition, the continuous development of Sino-American aviation affairs and the competition among various imperial powers for the development of aviation in the Far East have also been sufficient to promote the launch of this competition.

However, as soon as this world-shaking international aviation competition was completed, rumors of a second competition emerged. According to a Havas dispatch on the 26th, French Aviation Minister General Teran is also planning to organize an international aviation competition from Paris to Hanoi, Vietnam, a distance of 18,000 kilometers, not much different from the Anglo-Australian distance. The news has come, making people marvel at the world's enthusiasm for aviation. However, how can this be an exception? The intention is nothing more than to strengthen the relationship between French imperialism and its colonies in the Far East!

Marriage as a Child's Play 234

— Wen Bing

I read a divorce news item in the newspaper this morning, roughly as follows:

After Lawyer So-and-so married Miss So-and-so, they suddenly felt that their relationship was not harmonious and often quarreled, which led to the man filing a lawsuit for divorce in court. However, on the evening before the court hearing, the couple still lived together in an apartment and talked intimately. When they appeared in court the next day, they looked at each other and smiled. The lawyers representing both parties also said that they should not bother the court. As a result of the court hearing, the judge ordered them to go outside to reconcile and live together. The two parties looked at each other and smiled again and left the court together.

The performance of this fact is really inexplicable! The news reporter laughed so hard that their intestines were tied in knots, saying that it broke the divorce record. The author also laughed so hard that their skin was aching when they saw this news item, which was both humorous and meaningful, so I specifically brought it up for discussion.

Page 18

Since the founding of the Republic of China, the transition from arranged marriages to free marriages has been a good phenomenon. Although some conservative people are still stroking their beards and sighing, in general, most of the enlightened men and women are happy and diligently practice it. Its position has been established in law and in social customs.

However, perhaps because the change was too sudden, it resulted in the problem of overcorrection. The number of marital disputes in the past 20 years is indeed more than the total number accumulated in the previous thousands of years. This is not nonsense, but a completely true fact. It is common to be intimate and loving today and divorced and strangers tomorrow. Coming is convenient, and leaving is easy. This is the natural trend. Because there are so many disputes, people have doubts about the freedom of marriage itself, thinking that it is better to have arranged marriages than to have such disputes.

In fact, this is a complete misunderstanding. We should know that the reason why there are so many disputes in modern Chinese marriages is not the fault of marriage freedom itself, but the improper use of it. Nowadays, people simply regard marriage as a child's play, without any sincerity. They just want to have an affair and make friends, without making a pure observation of the other party, only relying on wealth and beauty. After marriage, they do not fulfill their marital obligations, considerateness, and tenderness. In this way, of course, it is easy to get together, easy to divorce, and there are endless disputes.

Although marriages in the Soviet Union are very common, with unions and divorces being nothing unusual, we cannot learn that kind of example after all, because our society is still a century apart. Everyone there has a job, and men and women have achieved true equality. Women also have economic autonomy and can move independently in society. Of course, getting together or divorcing doesn't matter. On the other hand, in our country, women are still as unable to be independent as in the past, relying entirely on their appearance to maintain their lives. When marriage becomes a child's play, it is the women who suffer.

The anecdote about Lawyer So-and-so and Miss So-and-so's divorce is the best example of marriage as a child's play. I hope that in this era of transition, everyone should be more aware of this. This is also a driving force for the development of return to normalcy.

No Way to Appeal 235

— Mu Feng

I saw a picture in a pictorial magazine titled "No Way to Appeal," a picture of disaster victims: more than a thousand old, young, women, and children disaster victims from Jiaxing, forced by hunger, gathered at the county government to beg for relief. The county government closed the iron gate tightly, and the disaster victims could not enter, so they sat outside the gate, waiting on empty stomachs.

It is said that this year's disaster situation is even worse than the major flood disaster in seven provinces in the 20th year of the Republic of China. Now, the northern provinces are flooded, and houses are in ruins. The southern provinces are barren land for thousands of miles, and crops are withered. The total loss from such water and drought disasters is more than 100 million yuan, and the disaster area accounts for two-thirds of the total area of the country.

Under the development of this natural law of society, the increasing bankruptcy of the rural economy has become an inevitable trend. What's more, now there is an additional layer of heavy disasters? Therefore, we can always see telegrams from various places begging for relief in the newspapers every day, knowing how the people in the disaster areas are crawling on the line of death and struggling with hunger and cold!

Although the various provincial drought relief associations have come up with a solution for the suffering of these tens of thousands of living beings. They have decided to raise donations from all sectors of society on the one hand and ask the central government to issue an order to implement relief by work and reduce and exempt land taxes and surcharges in the disaster-stricken areas on the other hand. However, these are not fundamental ways to save the disaster victims from their suffering. What's more, distant water cannot put out a nearby fire? I remember someone sighed and said: In the present time of scientific prosperity, we have no ability to resist the infringement of nature, and the extent of human affairs is unknowable! If we want to seek relief, in addition to treating the symptoms, we should also focus on treating the root causes. Otherwise, providing relief after the disaster is just a routine matter, even more shortsighted than treating the headache when the head hurts and treating the foot when the foot hurts. These words are the truth.

Writing to this point, the disaster victims, a group of over a thousand old, young, women, and children disaster victims, sitting on empty stomachs outside the iron gate of the county government, fully tasting the closed-door soup, are reflected in my eyes again. What a tragic scene of disaster victims crawling on the line of death and having no way to appeal!

A Country Child and a City Young Master

East, West, South, North 236

— San Duo

Sure enough, the joint conference of Shanghai universities has decided to strictly prohibit university students from entering dance halls to dance. This Japanese gossip news was actually adopted by the university federation, which was something that university students did not expect.

The question itself lies in why university students are prohibited from dancing? The news from both China and foreign countries is vague, and university students are prohibited from dancing for no reason.

Some time ago, dancing was used as a tool to save the country, which shows that dancing itself is not a despicable thing. However, the image of university students dancing is not good, so prohibiting university students from dancing is undoubtedly justified. University students themselves have to take responsibility for this, and we don't need to say much.

But can middle school students dance? Can elementary school students dance?

To 237

— Luo Shan

"Ah, my dear, have I offended you?" You shake your head, but answer with depression. Do you know that there is ten thousand times more sadness than yours in my heart!

"You are a talented poet, like Xiang Lun and Shelley, created by electricity. If it weren't for your beautiful spring, I'm afraid I would wither immediately!"

(That's not true!)

Dark haze flashes before my eyes, and the air is filled with the atmosphere of sorrow. I don't know why, but when you happily talk animatedly, you give me vitality, and when you are thoughtful and sad, you add such great pain to me!

(Your sorrows and joys are my sorrows and joys!)

I lightly lick my lips with the tip of my tongue.

What exactly am I giving you?

I understand that to be loved by someone is to give that person pain, I sigh.

You have always been a silent poet. The ideal world in your mind is so beautiful, with cherry blossoms everywhere. But reality has given you too many surprises! You are not happy, and you can't even say ten sentences a day.

I understand many of the pains in your heart that are difficult to express. Listen to the beating of my heart! Look at me—my dear, these heavy footsteps and locked eyebrows, and the fact that I haven't been able to sleep or eat well for so many days, please observe. I really love you too much, I am in pain, do you understand?

How long is life? We are spending this time so unhappily, so painfully, and every moment feels like a piece of red-hot tin melting into my heart. Tell me frankly, my dear, your depression is the same as mine.

(Eliminate me!)

Pressing against your body, my tilted head rests on your shoulder, full of crystal tears.

(……) Shaking your head, you grasp my hand tightly. My hands in August feel as cold as if a northwest wind has blown in the middle of winter.

Finally, we came back together in a third-class carriage. Your heart and my heart are so restless, beating wildly, almost jumping out of our chests. The result of waiting, anxiously waiting, is the restlessness of both parties. When you secretly look at me working alone at my desk, my hand wipes away the traces of tears.

(You belong to me, no matter how my life changes!)

I think in my heart and write it down on paper. Ah, my dear, this grand gift has made me feel dazed and uneasy for several days. I am ashamed. If you and I had met four years ago, I believe you would definitely love me a thousand times more. You can create many magical, touching poems, novels, great, and world-famous works of literature.

Page 19

The broken heart simply cannot bear this grand gift from you!

How can I not be sad? My dear, how can these two candle-like lives easily, easily melt into a delicate, exquisite

How can they easily melt into a delicate and exquisite thing—my dear, do you understand? If your eyes even glance at another pair, my heart beats so wildly that I simply want to escape into the earth immediately!

(You walk away with sorrow, your face is so pale, your eyes show fatigue, fatigue from life!)

I am restless, I live in an restless environment.

Analysis of the Family 238

— Wang Ren

The meaning of the word "family" has always referred to the place where people grow up and live: a collection of great-grandparents, brothers, nephews, sisters-in-law, wives, children, and grandchildren is what makes a family. To put it more clearly, it is said that what is within the doors, is a family. This is what is called a family.

Furthermore, according to the definition of the word: A woman asks her husband to be the head of the family. Therefore, Mencius said: When a girl is born, she wishes to have a family. At the same time, the word "family" can be interpreted the same as the word "姑" (father's sister/aunt): therefore, women can all be called "family." And what is called "大家" (dajia/great family) is also a respectful way of addressing women: as in the case of Ban Zhao of the Han Dynasty, who was called Cao Dajia, which is the reason for this.

If we extend the word "family" in a broader sense, the family, even in the past, was not so narrow. But in any case, the use of the word "family," although great, is not as rampant as it is today. Whenever they (the people of the past) applied the word "family," they would never go beyond the definition of being within the doors, so whether they said it horizontally or vertically, using it going and coming, the word "family" was ultimately used on the family, and would never be used outside the family.

If you don't believe me, let me give a few examples:

家人 (jia ren/family member): Similar to saying a person in the family.

家山 (jia shan/family mountain): It is what people now call their hometown.

家父 (jia fu/my father), 家母 (jia mu/my mother), 家兄 (jia xiong/my elder brother), 家姊 (jia zi/my elder sister)... are all humble terms used to refer to one's elders.

家廟 (jia miao/family temple): That is, the ancestral hall to which people in the countryside refer.

家事 (jia shi/family affairs): That is, the affairs of a family.

家計 (jia ji/family finances): That is, livelihood.

家法 (jia fa/family law): Used to restrain children, so as not to trouble the national government.

家賊 (jia zei/family thief): Refers to those unscrupulous real goods, who specialize in doing things that lead wolves into the house.

There are also 家書 (jia shu/family letters), 家訓 (jia xun/family precepts), 家學 (jia xue/family learning), 家聲 (jia sheng/family reputation)... the list is endless. In short, what was considered a family in the past was all within a doorframe, just like the women of the previous dynasty, who were not allowed to take a step out of the boudoir without singing loudly for liberation.

However, it is not the same now. Women have been liberated (?) and are equally free as men. Naturally, the application of a mere word, with the changes of the times, why can't it be broadened and generalized? Thus, the definition of the word "family" in modern society has become increasingly popular, expanding to the point where it cannot be expanded further, and generalizing to the point where it cannot be generalized further. From so-called politicians, jurists, educators, writers, artists,... anyone with a skill is a 家 (jia/expert). Thus, haircutting is a 家 (jia/profession), foot massage is a 家 (jia/profession), and masons and carpenters are also 家 (jia/profession), and peddlers are also 家 (jia/professional). Even more inferior, rickshaw pullers can become 家 (jia/professionals), and why can't righteous men alone be called 家 (jia/professionals)? Even vagrants, con men, beggars, and thieves can all be called 家 (jia/professionals). Thus, the meaning of the word "家" (jia/family/professional) is great! There is nothing that is not a 家 (jia/family/profession) in society, and the world is all 家 (jia/family/profession).

However, in this way, the initial definition of the word "family" is now completely reversed. What was previously a term within a door for a family has now broken out of the door limit and spread to society and all of humanity. I am afraid that even Confucius, when opening the dictionary, would be confused, and even if Cangjie were brought back, he would be dumbfounded!

Someone might say: This is one time, that is another. The narrow definition of the past does not suit the present. The idea of being within a door should be overthrown! Since the family can grow legs and walk all over the southeast, northwest, all over society, all over the world, and spread to everyone, it is a good thing. You should not be talking nonsense. I say: Yes, yes.

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments 240

Zhongxi (1040)

Yao Xiao'an, Pang Xueqing, Pearl Pagoda 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM Opening "Thinking of Melancholy"

When the fifth month arrives and pomegranates bloom, a young lady's heart is filled with longing. She longs to have two lovers, both handsome, romantic, and talented. The lovers' intentions are difficult to guess. They don't seem foolish or silent. Why do they come and go together, never speaking? Today, I, your humble servant, have nowhere to confide my true feelings. I am silently left with nothing to say. I contemplate indulging in romance, but with whom should I find joy, and whom should I abandon? This won't work, and that won't work. My heart is full of unspoken thoughts. If either of you gentlemen comes here in the future, please prepare fine food and wine on my behalf. Each handsome man should drink three cups of wine in my honor, and then reveal his true feelings. Let's not be jealous of each other but get along peacefully. The two lovers can alternate days, and when one doesn't come, the other will surely be here to fulfill my desires.

Huamei (1060)

Zhang Mengfei's Storytelling 4:45 PM to 5:30 PM

Opening Modern Men and Women

Society is open and values civilization. Men and women are all modern. Men despise traditional Chinese clothing and insist on Western suits and leather shoes. They hold a cane and wear pince-nez glasses. Women have permed, lion-like hair and walk lightly in high heels. They paint their eyebrows and apply lipstick. A smile turns heads and captivates souls. They stroll together in the park during the day and embrace in the dance hall at night. They watch movies in theaters and gamble at the jai alai court. Even more strangely, they can close themselves in a room for a moment and find satisfaction. Love doesn't need to be graded. Freedom is not hindered by shame. It's laughable how quickly they become husband and wife, and how easily they divorce. Such liberation is truly a joke; morality no longer exists. They must know that youth fades quickly, and every inch of time is precious. How can one waste their youth?

Chinese Classics 241

Huaxing (1260)

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Selected Tang Poems 9:00 AM to 9:30 AM

Spending the Night at Stone Moat Village, an Official Seizes People at Night, the Old Man Climbs Over the Wall and Flees,

The Old Woman Goes Out to Greet Him. The Official Shouts, How Angry! The Woman Cries, How Bitter!

Listening to the Woman's Words, Three Sons Were Stationed at Fengcheng, One Son Sent a Letter,

Two Sons Newly Died in Battle. The Surviving Ones Temporarily Steal Life, The Dead are Gone Forever.

There is No One Else in the Room, Only a Grandson at the Breast. The Grandson Has a Mother Who Has Not Left,

Her Skirt is Torn. Although the Old Woman is Feeble, She Asks to Return with the Official at Night,

To Quickly Respond to the Service at Heyang, and Still Be Able to Prepare the Morning Meal. After a Long Night, the Voices Cease,

As if Hearing Sobs. At Dawn, Setting Out on the Road Ahead, Parting Alone with the Old Man.

Drama 242

Zhongxi (1040)

Guanyin Society's Tale of Heroic Sons and Daughters 7:15 PM to 8:00 PM

An Xuehai, with the spirit of Guan Yu hanging up the gold seal, resigned from his official position,

and the whole family set out to visit the heroic woman in Renping!

Searching in West Village and East Village, she is not as good as Chu Yingxiong there!

At that moment, they met the old family servant Hua Zhong.

Yongsheng (1080)

Guanyin Society's Good Youth 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

Under the active efforts of Ms. Wan Wenjuan of the Frugality and Virtue Association, this is quite promising!

So pitiful! Zheng Fangyu still can't get any love from her, which is too hard!

Huamei (1060)

Guanyin Society's Laughable Fate 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM

The masquerade ball had not yet ended,

He Lina had already disappeared!

It was hard for this Commander Guang, who had fallen in love at first sight,

and he would also lose the pain of being lovelorn, him!

Xinsheng (1380)

Minsheng Drama Troupe's Leprous Woman 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM

In the mountain winds of Guangxi, women suffering from leprosy must first be touched by a man before they can be betrothed. Qiu Zimu, a wealthy man, had a daughter named Liyu, who was intelligent and beautiful. Suddenly, she contracted leprosy. Qiu asked his friend Shi Gonghun to find a traveler to touch his daughter. Chen Qiqin left home due to an incident and went to Guangxi to visit his uncle Huang Haike. On the way, he met a monk and learned that Haike had passed away. Chen Qiqin was stranded in a foreign land without finding relatives.
